Removed duplicates of file with Size: 123.511.024 bytes; 

$awk '!seen[$0]++' boot_success_b0x2f000000_addr_output_bigger.txt > boot_success_b0x2f000000_addr_output_bigger_cleaned.txt

This Files shows 'all' reads and writes during boot process that are:
> 0x2f000000

Beforehand it was observed that addresses from somewhere in that range are readed during the boot process, w/o beeing written from qemu;
By excluding certain addresses, it was possible to finally boot the kernel again with activated encryption;
